          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109"><label>4.24.109</label> śasyate triṣv api sadā vyāyāmo
            doṣanāśanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhuktaṃ viruddham apy annaṃ vyāyāmānna praduṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110"><label>4.24.110</label> utsargamaithunahāraśodhane syāt tu
            tanmanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             necched doṣacayāt prājñaḥ pīḍāṃ vā kāyamānasīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111"><label>4.24.111</label> atistrīsaṃprayogāc ca rakṣed ātmānam
            ātmavān |
            <caesura/>
             śūlakāsajvaraśvāsakārśyapāṇḍvāmayakṣayāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112"><label>4.24.112</label> ativyavājāj jāyante rogāś cākṣepakādayaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             āyuṣmanto mandajarā vapur varṇabalānvitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113"><label>4.24.113</label> sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti strīṣu
            saṃyatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tribhis tribhir ahobhir vā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"><label>4.24.114</label> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt pakṣād
            vrajed budhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rajasvalām akāmāṃ ca malinām apriyāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"><label>4.24.115</label> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā
            vyādhiprapīḍitām |
            <caesura/>
             hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116"><label>4.24.116</label> sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃ ca tathā pravrajitām
            api |
            <caesura/>
             sandhyāparvasvagamyāṃ ca nopeyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117"><label>4.24.117</label> gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā
            madhyandineṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte 'śuddha eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118"><label>4.24.118</label> kṣudhito vyādhitaś caiva kṣubdhacittaś ca
            mānavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātaviṇmūtravegī ca pipāsaratidurbalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119"><label>4.24.119</label> tiryagyonāv ayonau ca
            prāptaśukravidhāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭayonau visargaṃ tu balavān api varjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120"><label>4.24.120</label> retasaś cātimātraṃ tu mūrdhāvaraṇam eva
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             sthitāvuttānaśayane viśeṣeṇaiva garhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121"><label>4.24.121</label> krīḍāyām api medhāvī hitārthī
            parivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             rajasvalāṃ prāptavato narasyāniyatātmanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label>4.24.122</label> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hānir adharmaś ca tato
            bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrām atha parvasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label>4.24.123</label> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoś cāpi gacchato
            jīvitakṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label>4.24.124</label> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ
            vandhyāmasaṃvṛte |
            <caesura/>
             deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label>4.24.125</label> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaś ca madhyāhne
            tṛṣito 'balaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>4.24.126</label> atiprasaṅgād bhavati śoṣaḥ
            śukrakṣayāvahaḥ | vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyur mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>4.24.127</label> prayūṣasy ardharātre ca vātapitte
            prakupyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tiryagyonāv ayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>4.24.128</label> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ śukrasya ca
            kṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>4.24.129</label> uttāne ca bhavec chīghraṃ śukrāśmaryās tu
            saṃbhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaṃ pariharet tasmād etal lokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>4.24.130</label> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna sandhāryaṃ
            kathaṃcana |
            <caesura/>
             vayor ūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>4.24.131</label> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām
            alaṅkṛtām |
            <caesura/>
             seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>4.24.132</label> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ sasitaṃ rasa
            eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>4.24.133</label> mukhamātraṃ samāsena sadvṛttasyaitad
            īritam |
            <caesura/>
             ārogyam āyur artho vāg āsadbhiḥ prāpyate nṛbhiḥ ||</l>

            caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||24 ||</p>

          <head>ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>4.26.1</label> athātaḥ kṣīṇabalīyaṃ vājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"><label>4.26.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"><label>4.26.3</label> kalyasyodagravayaso vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarveṣv ṛtuṣv ahar ahar vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"><label>4.26.4</label> sthavirāṇāṃ riraṃsūnāṃ strīṇāṃ vāllabhyam
            icchatām |
            <caesura/>
             yoṣitprasaṅgāt kṣīṇānāṃ klībānām alparetasām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"><label>4.26.5</label> vilāsinām arthavatāṃ rūpayauvanaśālinām |
            <caesura/>
             nṛṇāṃ ca bahubhāryāṇāṃ yogā vājīkarā hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"><label>4.26.6</label> sevamāno yad aucity ād vājīvāty arthavegavān
            |
            <caesura/>
             nārīs tarpayate tena vājīkaraṇam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>4.26.7</label> bhojanāni vicitrāṇi pānāni vividhāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             vācaḥ śrotrānugāminyas tvacaḥ sparśasukhās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"><label>4.26.8</label> yāminī sendutilakā kāminī navayauvanā |
            <caesura/>
             gītaṃ śrotramanohāri tāmbūlaṃ madirāḥ srajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"><label>4.26.9</label> gandhā manojñā rūpāṇi citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             manasaś cāpratīghāto vājīkurvanti mānavam |
            <caesura/>
             tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>4.26.10</label> dveṣyastrīsaṃprayogāc ca klaibyaṃ tan
            mānasaṃ smṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭukāmloṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>4.26.11</label> saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaibyaṃ tad aparaṃ
            smṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             ativyavāyaśīlo yo na ca vājīkriyārataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"><label>4.26.12</label> dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti
            tacchukrakṣayahetukam |
            <caesura/>
             mahatā meḍhrarogeṇa marmacchedena vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"><label>4.26.13</label> klaibyam etac caturthaṃ syān nṝṇāṃ
            puṃstvopaghātajam |
            <caesura/>
             janmaprabhṛti yaḥ klībaḥ klaibyaṃ tat sahajaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"><label>4.26.14</label> balinaḥ kṣubdhamanaso nirodhād
            brahmacaryataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṣṭhaṃ klaibyaṃ mataṃ tat tu kharaśukranimittajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15"><label>4.26.15</label> asādhyaṃ sahajaṃ klaibyaṃ marmacchedāc ca
            yad bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             sādhyānām itareṣāṃ tu kāryo hetuviparyayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16"><label>4.26.16</label> vidhir vājīkaro yas tu taṃ pravakṣyāmy ataḥ
            param |
            <caesura/>
             tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ cūrṇam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17"><label>4.26.17</label> pauṇḍrakekṣurasairārdraṃ marditaṃ
            saindhavānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             varāhamedasā yuktāṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18"><label>4.26.18</label> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā puruṣo gacchet tu
            pramadāśatam |
            <caesura/>
             bastāṇḍasiddhe payasi bhāvitān asakṛt tilān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19"><label>4.26.19</label> śiśumāravasāpakvāḥ śaṣkulyastistailaiḥ
            kṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yaḥ svādet sa pumān gacchet strīṇāṃ śatam apūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20"><label>4.26.20</label> pippalīlavaṇopete bastāṇḍe kṣīrasarpiṣi |
            <caesura/>
             sādhite bhakṣayed yas tu sa gacchet pramadāśatam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21"><label>4.26.21</label> pippalīmāṣaśālīnāṃ yavagodhūmayos tathā |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇabhāgaiḥ samais tais tu ghṛte pūpalikāṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22"><label>4.26.22</label> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā tu śarkarāmadhuraṃ
            payaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             naraś caṭakavad gacched daśavārān nirantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23"><label>4.26.23</label> vidāryāḥ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ svarasenaiva
            bhāvitam |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhuyutaṃ līḍhvā daśa strīr adhigacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24"><label>4.26.24</label> evam āmalakaṃ cūrṇaṃ svarasenaiva bhāvitam
            |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāmadhusarpibhir yuktaṃ līḍhvā payaḥ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25"><label>4.26.25</label> etenāśītivarṣo 'pi yuveva parihṛṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīlavaṇopete bastāṇḍe ghṛtasādhite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26"><label>4.26.26</label> śiśumārasya vā khādet te tu vājīkare bhṛśam
            |
            <caesura/>
             kulīrakūrmanakrāṇām aṇḍāny evaṃ tu bhakṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27"><label>4.26.27</label> mahiṣarṣabhabastānāṃ pibec chukrāṇi vā
            naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aśvatthaphalamūlatvakśuṅgāsiddhaṃ payo naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.28"><label>4.26.28</label> pītvā saśarkarākṣaudraṃ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati
            |
            <caesura/>
             vidārimūlakalkaṃ tu śṛtena payasā naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.29"><label>4.26.29</label> uḍumbarasamaṃ pītvā vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate |
            <caesura/>
             māṣāṇāṃ palam ekaṃ tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30"><label>4.26.30</label> avalihya payaḥ pītvā tena vājī bhaven naraḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīrapakvāṃs tu godhūmān ātmaguptāphalaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.31"><label>4.26.31</label> śītān ghṛtayutān khādet tataḥ paś cāt payaḥ
            pibet |
            <caesura/>
             nakramūṣikamaṇḍūkacaṭakāṇḍakṛtaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.32"><label>4.26.32</label> pādābhyaṅgena kurute balaṃ bhūmiṃ tu na
            spṛśet |
            <caesura/>
             yāvat spṛśati no bhūmiṃ tāvad gacchen nirantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.33"><label>4.26.33</label> svayaṃguptekṣurakayoḥ phalacūrṇaṃ
            saśarkaram |
            <caesura/>
             dhāroṣṇena naraḥ pītvā payasā na kṣayaṃ vrajet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34"><label>4.26.34</label> uccaṭācūrṇaṃ peyam evaṃ balārthinā |
            <caesura/>
             svayaṃguptāphalair yuktaṃ māṣasūpaṃ piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.35"><label>4.26.35</label> guptāphalaṃ gokṣurakāc ca bījaṃ tathoccaṭāṃ
            gopayasā vipācya |
            <caesura/>
             khajāhataṃ śarkarayā ca yuktaṃ pītvā naro hṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"><label>4.26.36</label> māṣān vidārīm api soccaṭāṃ ca kṣīre gavāṃ
            kṣaudraghṛtopapannām |
            <caesura/>
             pītvā naraḥ śarkarayā suyuktāṃ kuliṅgavad dhṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.37"><label>4.26.37</label> gṛṣṭīnāṃ vṛddhavatsānāṃ māṣaparṇabhṛtāṃ
            gavām |
            <caesura/>
             yat kṣīraṃ tat praśaṃsanti balakāmeṣu jantuṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.38"><label>4.26.38</label> kṣīramāṃsagaṇāḥ sarve kākolyādiś ca pūjitaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             vājīkaraṇahetor hi tasmāt tut tu prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.39"><label>4.26.39</label> ete vājīkarā yogāḥ prītyapatyabalapradāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sevyā viśuddhopacitadehaiḥ kālādyapekṣayā ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ kṣīṇabalīyavājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||26 ||</p>

        <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"><label>4.28.1</label> athāto medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ<ref
              rend="superscript footnote
       marker">*</ref> vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"><label>4.28.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"><label>4.28.3</label> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ
            śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya
            snehakumbhe saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau nidadhyāt, saptarātrāduddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya
            yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacched anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet;
            bhallātakavidhānavaccāgārapraveśaḥ, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe himābhir adbhiḥ
            pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca payasā śarkarāmadhureṇaudanamaśnīyāt; evaṃ
            ṣaṇmāsānupayujya vigatapāpmā balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur
            bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ pāṇḍurogiṇamudariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā gormūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ
            vigatalauhity e savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam
            aśnīyāt, evaṃ māsamupayujya smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati |
            eṣaevopayogaścitrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś ca; citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ paraṃ
            pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"><label>4.28.4</label> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
            yathākramamāgāraṃ praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ yavānnaṃ
            payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayet trīn māsān payo 'nupānaṃ, jīrṇe payaḥ
            sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī śrutanigādī bhavati
            varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātramenāṃ bhakṣayet, trirātrādūrdhvaṃ
            payaḥ sarpiriti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ piṇḍaṃ vā payasā++āloḍya pibet, evaṃ
            dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"><label>4.28.5</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalampayuñjīta, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet, kṣīrasātmyo vā payasā
            bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī medhāvī bhavati, dvitīyaṃ saptarātram
            upayujya granthamīpsitamutpādayati naṣṭaṃ cāsya prādurbhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram
            upayujya dviruccāritaṃ śatamapyavadhārayati, evam ekaviṃśatirātram
            upayujyālakṣmīrapakrāmati; mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevyanupraviśati, sarvāś cainaṃ śrutaya
            upatiṣṭhanti, śrutadharaḥ pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"><label>4.28.6</label> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprasthaṃ
            viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayor dvādaśa harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni
            ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tataḥ pūrvavidhānena
            mātrāṃ yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, pūrvavaccātra
            parīhāraḥ, etenordhvamadhastiryak kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīrapakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ
            sthiravayāḥ śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyurbhavati; etad eva
            kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu saṃśodhanamādiśanti
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"><label>4.28.7</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ
            piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ,
            evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ vivriyate, dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān
            bhavati, trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte, caturdvādaśarātram upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ,
            tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate, śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya
            pibet payasā, samānaṃ bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"><label>4.28.8</label> vacāśatapākaṃ vā sarpirdroṇam upayujya
            pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati, galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃś cāpahantīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"><label>4.28.9</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi āyuṣkāmarasāyanam |
            <caesura/>
             mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"><label>4.28.10</label> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ vārān
            sahasraśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"><label>4.28.11</label> sarpirmdhuyutaṃ lihyādalakṣmīnāśanaṃ param
            |
            <caesura/>
             tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"><label>4.28.12</label> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā hutvā
            samāhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             daśasāhassramāyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"><label>4.28.13</label> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu madhulājaiś ca
            saṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"><label>4.28.14</label> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ
            priyaṅgavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gavyena payasā pītamalakṣmīṃ pratibedhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"><label>4.28.15</label> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena payasā śṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdhamalakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"><label>4.28.16</label> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca
            mākṣikam |
            <caesura/>
             pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"><label>4.28.17</label> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca bilvacūrṇam iti trayam
            |
            <caesura/>
             medhyamāyuṣyamārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"><label>4.28.18</label> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailamāvāpya sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             hutvā sahasramaśnīyānmedhyamāyuṣyamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"><label>4.28.19</label> yāvakāṃstāvakān khādedabhibhūya yavāṃs
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavadbhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"><label>4.28.20</label> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇam iti ca trayam
            |
            <caesura/>
             prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"><label>4.28.21</label> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyagupayuktaṃ dine dine |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayed vaśe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"><label>4.28.22</label> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ mākṣikaṃ madhu
            |
            <caesura/>
             suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyamicchatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"><label>4.28.23</label> padmanīlotpalakvāthe yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirāsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā paibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"><label>4.28.24</label> payaś cānupibet siddhaṃ teṣām eva
            samudbhave |
            <caesura/>
             alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā++āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"><label>4.28.25</label> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣveteṣu sādhane |
            <caesura/>
             śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"><label>4.28.26</label> pāpmānaṃ nāśayantyetā dadyuś cauṣadhayaḥ
            śriyam |
            <caesura/>
             kuryurnāgabalaṃ cāpi manuṣyamamaropamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"><label>4.28.27</label> satatādhyayanaṃ vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanam |
            <caesura/>
             tadvidyācāryasevā ca buddhimedhākaro guṇaḥ(gaṇaḥ) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"><label>4.28.28</label> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ cāvidhāraṇam
            |
            <caesura/>
             brahmacaryamahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
            nāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||28 ||</p>

        <div n="29" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"><label>4.29.1</label> athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ
            rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"><label>4.29.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3"><label>4.29.3</label> brahmādayo 'sṛjan pūrvam amṛtaṃ somasaṃjñitam
            |
            <caesura/>
             jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4"><label>4.29.4</label> eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ
            sthānanāmākṛtivīryaviśeṣaiś caturviṃśatidhābhidyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5"><label>4.29.5</label> aṃśumān muñjavāṃś caiva candramā
            rajataprabhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dūrvāsomaḥ kanīyāṃś ca śvetākṣaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6"><label>4.29.6</label> pratānavāṃstālavṛntaḥ karavīro 'ṃśavān api |
            <caesura/>
             svayaṃprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"><label>4.29.7</label> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ śākvaras
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             agniṣṭomo raivataś ca yathokta iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8"><label>4.29.8</label> gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaś coḍupatir ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nām abhiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9"><label>4.29.9</label> sarveṣām eva caiteṣām eko vidhir upāsane |
            <caesura/>
             sarve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10"><label>4.29.10</label> ato 'nyatamaṃ somam upayuyukṣuḥ
            sarvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ praśaste deśe trivṛtam āgāraṃ kārayitvā hṛtadoṣaḥ
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu aṃśumantam
            ādāyādhvarakalpenāhṛtam abhiṣutam abhihutaṃ cāntarāgāre kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaḥ
            somakandaṃ suvarṇasūcyā vidārya payo gṛhṇīyāt sauvarṇe (<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>rājate vā) pātre 'ñjalimātraṃ, tataḥ sakṛd
            evopayuñjīta nāsvādayan, tata upaspṛśya śeṣam apsv avasādya yamaniyamābhyām ātmānaṃ
            saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantarataḥ suhṛdbhir upāsyamāno viharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11"><label>4.29.11</label> rasāyanaṃ pītavāṃs tu nivāte tanmanāḥ śuciḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             āsīta tiṣṭhet krāmec ca na kathaṃcana saṃviśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12"><label>4.29.12</label> sāyaṃ vā bhuktavān upaśrutaśāntiḥ
            kuśaśayyāyāṃ kṛṣṇājinottarāyāṃ suhṛdbhir upāsyamānaḥ śayīta, tṛṣito vā śītodakamātrāṃ
            pibet (aśanāyito vā kṣīraṃ); tataḥ prātar utthāyopaśrutaśāntiḥ kṛtamaṅgalo gāṃ spṛṣṭvā
            tatahaivāsīta, tasya jīrṇe some chardir utpadyate, tataḥ śoṇitāktaṃ kṛmivyāmiśraṃ
            charditavate sāyaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ kṣīraṃ vitaret; tatas tṛtīye 'hani kṛmivyāmiśram
            atisāryate, sa tenāniṣṭapratigrahabhuktaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair vinirmuktaḥ śuddhatanur
            bhavati, tataḥ sāyaṃ snātāya pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ vitaret, kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ cainaṃ
            śayyāyāṃ śāyayet; tataś caturthe 'hani tasya śvayathur utpadyate, tataḥ sarvāṅgebhyaḥ
            kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tadahaś ca śayyāyāṃ pāṃśubhir avakīryamāṇaḥ śayīta, tataḥ sāyaṃ
            pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ vitaret; evaṃ pañcamaṣaṣṭhayor divasayor varteta, kevalam
            ubhayakālam asmai kṣīraṃ vitaret; tataḥ saptame 'hani nirmāṃsas tv agasthibhūtaḥ kevalaṃ
            somaparigrahād evocchvasiti, tad ahaś ca kṣīreṇa sukhoṣṇena pariṣicya
            tilamadhukacandanānuliptadehaṃ payaḥ pāyayet; tato 'ṣṭame 'hani prātar eva
            kṣīrapariṣiktaṃ candanapradigdhāgātraṃ payaḥ pāyayitvā pāṃśuśayyāṃ samutsṛjya
            kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet, tato 'sya māṃsam āpyāyyate, tvak cāvadalati,
            dantanakharomāṇi cāsya patanti; tasya navamadivasāt prabhṛty aṇutailābhyaṅgaḥ
            somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ; tato daśame 'hany etad eva vitaret, tato 'sya tvak sthiratām
            upaiti; evam ekādaśadvādaśayor varteta; tatas trayodaśāt prabhṛti
            somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ, evam āṣoḍaśād varteta; tataḥ saptadaśāṣṭādaśayor divasayor
            daśanā jāyante śikhariṇaḥ snigdhavajravaidūryasphaṭikaprakāśāḥ samāḥ sthirāḥ sahiṣṇavaḥ,
            tadā prabhṛti cānavaiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ kṣīrayavāgūm upaseveta yāvat pañcaviṃśatiriti; tato
            'smai dadyāc chālyodanaṃ mṛdūbhayakālaṃ payasā, tato 'sya nakhā jāyante
            vidrumendragopakataruṇādity aprakāśāḥ, sthirāḥ snigdhā lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ keśāś ca sūkṣmā
            jāyante, tvak ca nīlotpalātasīpuṣpavaidūryaprakāśā; ūrdhvaṃ ca māsāt keśān vāpayet,
            vāpayitvā cośīracandanakṛṣṇatilakalkaiḥ śiraḥ pradihyāt payasā vā snāpayet; tato
            'syānantaraṃ saptarātrāt keśā jāyante bhramarāñjananibhāḥ kuñcitāḥ sthirāḥ snigdhāḥ;
            tatas trirātrāt prathamāvasathaparisarān niṣkramya muhūrtaṃ sthitvā punar evāntaḥ
            praviśet, tato 'sya balātailam abhyaṅgārthe 'vacāryaṃ, yavapiṣṭam udvartanārthe,
            sukhoṣṇaṃ ca payaḥ pariṣekārthe, ajakarṇakaṣāyam utsādanārthe, sośīraṃ kūpodakaṃ
            snānārthe, candanam anulepārthe, āmalakarasavimiśrāś cāsya yūṣasūpavikalpāḥ,
            kṣīramadhukasiddhaṃ ca kṛṣṇatilam avacāraṇārthe, evaṃ daśarātraṃ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ
            dvitīye parisare varteta; tatas tṛtīye parisare sthirīkurvann ātmānam anyaddaśarātram
            āsīta, kiñcid ātapapavanān vā seveta, punaś cāntaḥ praviśet, na cātmānam ādarśe 'psu vā
            nirīkṣeta rūpaśālitvāt ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ krodhādīn pariharet, evaṃ sarveṣām
            upayogavikalpaḥ | viśeṣatas tu vallīpratānakṣupakādayaḥ somā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyair
            bhakṣayitavyāḥ | teṣāṃ tu pramāṇam ardhacatuṣkamuṣṭayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13"><label>4.29.13</label> aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇe pātre 'bhiṣuṇuyāt,
            candramasaṃ rājate; tāv upayujyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyeśānaṃ devam anupraviśati,
            śeṣāṃs tu tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā rohite vā carmaṇi vitate; śūdravarjaṃ tribhir varṇaiḥ
            somā upayoktavyāḥ | tataś caturthe māse paurṇamāsyāṃ śucau deśe brāhmaṇānarcayitvā
            kṛtamaṅgalo niṣkramya yathoktaṃ vrajed iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14"><label>4.29.14</label> oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujya vicakṣaṇaḥ |

             daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navāṃ dhārayate tanum || </l>

        <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.1"><label>4.32.1</label> athātaḥ svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.2"><label>4.32.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.3"><label>4.32.3</label> caturvidhaḥ svedaḥ tad yathā tāpasveda,
            ūṣmasveda, upanāhasvedo, dravasveda iti atra sarvasvedavikalpāvarodhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.4"><label>4.32.4</label> tatra tāpasvedaḥ
            pāṇikāṃsyakandukakapālavālukāvastraiḥ prayujyate, śayānasya cāṅgatāpo bahuśaḥ
            khādirāṅgārair iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.5"><label>4.32.5</label> ūṣmasvedastu
            kapālapāṣāśeṣṭakālohapiṇḍānagnivarṇānadbhir āsiñcedamladravyair vā,
            tairārdrālaktakapariveṣṭitair aṅgapradeśaṃ svedayet |
            māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmlavātaharapatrabhaṅgakvāthapūrṇāṃ vā kumbhīmanutaptāṃ
            prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa vā kumbhenādhomukhena tasyā mukham abhis
            andhāya tasmiñchidrehastiśuṇḍākārāṃ nāḍīṃ praṇidhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.6"><label>4.32.6</label> sukhopaviṣṭaṃ svabhyaktaṃ guruprāvaraṇāvṛtam
            |
            <caesura/>
             hastiśuṇḍikayā nāḍyā svedayed vātarogiṇam | sukhā sarvāṅgagā hyeṣā na ca kliśnāti
            mānavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.7"><label>4.32.7</label> vyāmārdhamātrā trirvakrā hastihastasamākṛtiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             svedanārthe hitā nāḍī kailiñjī hastiśuṇḍikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8ab"><label>4.32.8</label> puruṣāyāmamātrāṃ ca bhūmimutkīrya khādiraiḥ
            | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8cd">kāṣṭhair dagdhvā tathā 'bhyukṣya kṣīradhānyāmlavāribhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.9"><label>4.32.9</label> patrabhaṅgair avacchādya śayānaṃ svedayet
            tataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvavat svedayed dagdhvā bhasmāpohyāpi vā śilām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.10"><label>4.32.10</label> pūrvavat kuṭīṃ vā caturdvārāṃ kṛtvā tasyām
            upaviṣṭasyāntaś caturdvāre 'ṅgārānupasandhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.11"><label>4.32.11</label> kośadhānyāni vā samyagupasvedyāstīrya
            kiliñje 'nyasmin vā tatpratirūpake śayānaṃ prāvṛtya svedayet; evaṃ
            pāṃśugośakṛttuṣabusapalāloṣm abhiḥ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.12"><label>4.32.12</label> upanāhasvedas tu vātaharamūlakalkair
            amlapiṣṭair lavaṇapragāḍhaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ pradihya svedayet | evaṃ
            kākolyādibhir elādibhiḥ surasādibhis tilātasīsarṣapakalkaiḥ kṛśarāpāyasotkārikābhir
            veśavāraiḥ sālvaṇair vā tanuvastrāvanaddhaiḥ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.13"><label>4.32.13</label> dravasvedas tu vātaharadravyakvāthapūrṇe
            koṣṇakaṭāhe droṇyāṃ vā 'vagāhya svedayet, evaṃ
            payomāṃsarasayūṣatailadhānyāmlaghṛtavasāmūtreṣv avagāheta; etair eva <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>sukhoṣṇaiḥ kaṣāyaiś ca pariṣiñcediti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.14"><label>4.32.14</label> tatra tāpoṣmasvedau viśeṣataḥ śleṣmaghnau,
            upanāhasvedo vātaghnaḥ, anyatarasmin pittasaṃsṛṣṭe dravasveda iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.15"><label>4.32.15</label> kaphamedonvite vāyau
            nivātātapaguruprāvaraṇaniyuddhādhvavyāyāmabhāraharaṇāmarṣaiḥ svedamutpādayed iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.16"><label>4.32.16</label> bhavanti cātra caturvidho yo 'bhihito
            dvidhā svedaḥ prayujyate |
            <caesura/>
             sarvasminn eva dehe tu dehasyāvayave tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.17"><label>4.32.17</label> yeṣāṃ nasyaṃ vidhātavyaṃ bastiś caiva hi
            dehinām |
            <caesura/>
             śodhanīyāś ca ye kecit pūrvaṃ svedyās tu te matāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.18"><label>4.32.18</label> paś cāt svedyā hṛte śalye mūḍhagarbhā
            'nupadravā |
            <caesura/>
             samyak prajātā kāle yā paś cāt svedyā vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.19"><label>4.32.19</label> svedyaḥ pūrvaṃ ca paś cācca
            bhagandaryarśasas tathā |
            <caesura/>
             aśmaryā cāturo jantuḥ śeṣāñchāstre pracakṣmahe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.20"><label>4.32.20</label> nānabhyakte nāpi cāsnigdhadehe svedo yojyaḥ
            svedavidbhiḥ kathañcit |
            <caesura/>
             dṛṣṭaṃ loke kāṣṭhamasnigdhamāśu gacchedbhaṅgaṃ svedayogair gṛhītam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.21"><label>4.32.21</label> snehaklinnā dhātusaṃsthāś ca doṣāḥ
            svasthānasthā ye ca mārgeṣu līnāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             samyak svedair yojitais te dravatvaṃ prāptāḥ koṣṭhaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śodhanair yāntyaśeṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.22"><label>4.32.22</label> agnerdīptiṃ mārdavaṃ tvakprasādaṃ
            bhaktaśraddhāṃ srotasāṃ nirmalatvam |
            <caesura/>
             kuryāt svedo hanti nidrāṃ satandrāṃ sandhīn stabdhāṃśceṣṭayed āśu yuktaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.23"><label>4.32.23</label> svedāsrāvo vyādhihānirlaghutvaṃ
            śītārthitvaṃ mārdavaṃ cāturasya |
            <caesura/>
             samyaksvinne lakṣaṇaṃ prāhuretanmithyāsvinne vyatyayenaitad eva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.24"><label>4.32.24</label> svinne 'tyarthaṃ sandhipīḍā vidāhaḥ
            sphoṭotpattiḥ pittaraktaprakopaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchā bhrāntirdāhatṛṣṇe klamaś ca kuryāt tūrṇaṃ tatra śītaṃ vidhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.25"><label>4.32.25</label> pāṇḍurmehī pittaraktī kṣayārtaḥ kṣāmo
            'jīrṇī codarārto viṣārtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛḍcchardyārto garbhiṇī pītamadyo naite svedyā yaś ca martyo<ref
              rend="superscript footnote
          marker">*</ref>atisārī |
            <caesura/>
             svedādeṣāṃ yānti dehā vināśaṃ nosādhyatvaṃ yānti caiṣāṃ vikārāḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             svedaiḥ sādhyo durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaḥ syātāṃ ceddvau svedanīyau tatastau |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.26"><label>4.32.26</label>
            <caesura/>
             eteṣāṃ svedasādhyā ye vyādhayas teṣu buddhimān |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdūn svedān prayuñjīta tathā hṛnmuṣkadṛṣṭiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.27"><label>4.32.27</label> sarvān svedānnivāte ca jīrṇānnasyāvacārayet
            |
            <caesura/>
             snehābhyaktaśarīrasya śītairācchādya cakṣuṣī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.28"><label>4.32.28</label> svidyamānasya ca muhurhṛdayaṃ śītalaiḥ
            spṛśet |
            <caesura/>
             samyaksvinnaṃ vimṛditaṃ snātamuṣṇāmbubhiḥ śanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29ab"><label>4.32.29</label> svabhyaktaṃ prāvṛtāṅgaṃ ca
            nivātaśaraṇasthitam | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29cd">bhojayed anabhiṣyandi sarvaṃ cācāram ādiśet ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ nāma
            dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32 ||</p>

        <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
          <head>trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1"><label>4.33.1</label> athāto vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"><label>4.33.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3"><label>4.33.3</label> doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ, kupitāḥ
            praśamayitavyāḥ, vṛddhā nirhartavyāḥ, samāḥ paripālyā iti siddhāntaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4"><label>4.33.4</label> prādhānyena vamanavirecane vartate nirharaṇe
            doṣāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt tayor vidhānam ucyamānam upadhāraya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5"><label>4.33.5</label> athāturaṃ snigdhaṃ svinnam abhiṣyandibhir
            āhārair anavabaddhadoṣamavalokya śvo vamanaṃ pāyayitā 'smīti saṃbhojayet tīkṣṇāgniṃ
            balavantaṃ bahudoṣaṃ mahāvyādhiparītaṃ vamanasātmyaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6"><label>4.33.6</label> bhavati cātra peśalair vividhair annair
            doṣānutkleśya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7"><label>4.33.7</label> athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe sādhāraṇe kāle
            vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇasnehānām anyatamasya mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayed yathāyogaṃ
            koṣṭhaviśeṣamavekṣya; asātmyabībhatsadurgandhadurdarśanāni ca vamanāni vidadhyāt, ato
            viparītāni virecanāni; tatra sukumāraṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ bhīruṃ vā vamanasādhyeṣu
            vikāreṣu kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayet, pītauṣadhaṃ ca pāṇibhir
            agnitaptaiḥ pratāpyamānaṃ muhūrtamupekṣeta; tasya ca svedaprādurbhāveṇa
            śithilatāmāpannaṃ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ pracalitaṃ kukṣimanusṛtaṃ jānīyāt, tataḥ
            pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭamāptair lalāṭe pṛṣṭhe pārśvayoḥ kaṇṭhe ca
            pāṇibhiḥ suparigṛhītamaṅgulīgandharvahastotpalanālānām anyatamena kaṇṭham abhis pṛśantaṃ
            vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8"><label>4.33.8</label> bhavataś cātra kaphaprasekaṃ hṛdyāviśuddhiṃ
            kaṇḍūṃ ca duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittātiyogaṃ ca cisaṃjñatāṃ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9"><label>4.33.9</label> pitte kaphasyānu sukhaṃ pravṛtte śuddheṣu
            hṛtkaṇṭhaśiraḥsu cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10"><label>4.33.10</label> samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis amīkṣya
            snehanavirecanaśamanānāṃ dhūmānām anyatamaṃ sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā++ācārikam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11"><label>4.33.11</label> bhavanti cātra tato 'parāhṇe
            śuciśuddhadehamuṣṇābhir addbhiḥ pariṣiktagātram |
            <caesura/>
             kulatthamudgāḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yūṣai rasair vā 'pyupabhojayet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12"><label>4.33.12</label>
            kāsopalepasvarabhedanidrātandrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaphaprasekagrahaṇīpradoṣā na santi jantorvamataḥ kadācit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13"><label>4.33.13</label> chinne tarau puṣpaphalaprarohā yathā
            vināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti |
            <caesura/>
             tathā hṛte śleṣmaṇi śodhanena tajjā vikārāḥ praśamaṃ prayānti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14"><label>4.33.14</label> na vāmayet
              taimirikordhvavātagulmodaraplīhakṛmiśramārtān<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> |
            <caesura/>
             sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhamūtrāturān kevalavātarogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15"><label>4.33.15</label>
            svaropaghātādhyayanaprasaktaduśchardiduḥkoṣṭhatṛḍārtabālām |
            <caesura/>
             ūrdhvāsrapittikṣudhitātirūkṣagarbhiṇyudāvartirūhitāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"><label>4.33.16</label> avamyavamanādrogāḥ kṛcchratāṃ yānti dehinām
            |
            <caesura/>
             asādhyatāṃ vā gacchanti naite vāmyāstataḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17"><label>4.33.17</label> ete 'pyajīrṇavyathitā vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             atīva colbaṇakaphāste ca syur madhukāmbunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"><label>4.33.18</label> vāmyāstu
            viṣaśoṣastanyadoṣamandāgnyunmādāpasmāraślīpadārbudavidārikāmedomehagarajvarārucyapacyāmātīsārahṛdrogacittavibhramavisarpavidradhyajīrṇamukhaprasekahṛllāsaśvāsakāsapīnasapūtīnāsakaṇṭhauṣṭhavaktrapākakarṇasrāvādhijihvopajihvikāgalaśuṇḍikādhaḥśoṇitapittinaḥ
            kaphasthānajeṣu vikāreṣv anye ca kaphavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19"><label>4.33.19</label> virecanam api snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca
            deyam; avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi sato 'dhaḥ srastaḥ śleṣmā grahaṇīṃ chādayati,
            gauravam āpādayati, pravāhikāṃ vā janayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20"><label>4.33.20</label> athāturaṃ śvo virecanaṃ pāyayitā 'smīti
            pūrvāhṇe laghu bhojayet , phalāmlamuṣṇodakaṃ cainamanupāyayet | athāpare 'hani
            vigataśleṣmadhātumāturopakramaṇīyādavekṣyāturamathāsmai auṣadhamātrāṃ pātuṃ prayacchet
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21"><label>4.33.21</label> tatra mṛduḥ, krūro, madhyama iti trividhaḥ
            koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto mṛduḥ, sa dugdhenāpi viricyate; bahuvātaśleṣmā krūraḥ,
            sa durvirecyaḥ; samadoṣo madhyamaḥ, sa sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau mātrā mṛdvī, tīkṣṇā
            krūre, madhye madhyā kartavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāśe virecyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"><label>4.33.22</label> virecanaṃ pītavāṃs tu na vegān dhārayed
            budhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nivātaśāyī śītāmbu na spṛśenna pravāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23"><label>4.33.23</label> yathā ca vamane
            prasekauṣadhakaphapittānilāḥ krameṇa gacchanti, evaṃ virecane
            mūtrapurīṣapittauṣadhakaphā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24"><label>4.33.24</label> bhavanti cātra hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ
            paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṅgāś ca na sadvirikte |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamaś cātiviriktaliṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25"><label>4.33.25</label> gateṣu doṣeṣu kaphānviteṣu nābhyā laghutve
            manasaś ca tuṣṭau |
            <caesura/>
             gate 'nile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ manujaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26"><label>4.33.26</label> mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na
            pāyayetāhani tatra peyām |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārtaṃ suvirecitaṃ ca tanvīṃ sukhoṣṇāṃ laghu pāyayec ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27"><label>4.33.27</label> buddheḥ prasādaṃ balamindiryāṇāṃ
            dhātusthiratvaṃ balamagnidīptim |
            <caesura/>
             cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28"><label>4.33.28</label> yathaudakānāmudake 'panīte carasthirāṇāṃ
            bhavati praṇāśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pitte hṛte tvevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmakānāṃ bhavati praṇāśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29"><label>4.33.29</label> mandāgnyatisnehitabālavṛddhasthūlāḥ
            kṣatakṣīṇabhayopataptāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrāntastṛṣārto 'parijīrṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya cāsṛk || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30"><label>4.33.30</label> navapraviśyāyamadātyayī ca navajravī yā ca
            navaprasūtā |
            <caesura/>
             śalyārditāś cāpy avirecanīyāḥ snehādibhir ye tvanupaskṛtāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31"><label>4.33.31</label> virecanair yānti narā vināśamajñaprayuktair
            avirecanīyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"><label>4.33.32</label> virecyās tu jvaragarārucyarśo
            'rbudodaragranthividradhipāṇḍurogāpasmārahṛdrogavātaraktabhagandaracchardiyonirogavisarpagulmapakvāśayarugvibandhavisūcikālasakamūtrāghātakuṣṭhavisphoṭakapramehānāhaplīhaśophavṛddhiśastrakṣatakṣārāgnidagdhaduṣṭavraṇākṣipākakācatimirābhiṣyandaśiraḥkarṇākṣināsāsyagudameḍhradāhordhvaraktapittakṛmikoṣṭhinaḥ
            pittasthānajeṣv anyeṣu ca vikāreṣv anye ca paittikavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33"><label>4.33.33</label> saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyauṣṇyavikāśitvair
            virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣaṃ prakṛtyā gatamanyathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34"><label>4.33.34</label> yātyadho doṣamādāya pacyamānaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             guṇotkarṣāhvrajatyūrdhvamapakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35"><label>4.33.35</label> mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgneratitīkṣṇaṃ virecanam
            |
            <caesura/>
             na samyaṅnirhareddoṣānativegapradhāvitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.36"><label>4.33.36</label> pītaṃ yadauṣadhaṃ prātar bhuktapākasame
            kṣaṇe |
            <caesura/>
             paktiṃ gacchati doṣāṃś ca nirharettat praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37"><label>4.33.37</label> durbalasya calān doṣānalpānalpān punaḥ
            punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             haret prabhūtānakpāṃs tu śamayet pracyutānapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38"><label>4.33.38</label> hareddoṣāṃś calān pakvān balino durbalasya
            vā |
            <caesura/>
             calā hy upekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuściraṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39"><label>4.33.39</label> mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhaṃ ca sakṣāralavaṇair
            ghṛtaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sandhukṣitāgniṃ snigdhaṃ ca svinnaṃ caiva virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40"><label>4.33.40</label> snigdhasvinnasya bhaiṣajyair
            doṣastūtkleśito balāt |
            <caesura/>
             nilīyate na mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa ivodakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41"><label>4.33.41</label> na cātisnehapītas tu pibet snehavirecanam |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ pracalitāḥ sthānādbhūyaḥ śliṣyanti vartmasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"><label>4.33.42</label> viṣābhighātapiḍakāśophapāṇḍuvisarpiṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nātisnigdhā viśodhyāḥ syus tathā kuṣṭhipramehiṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43"><label>4.33.43</label> virūkṣya snehasātmyaṃ tu bhūyaḥ saṃsnehya
            śodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tena doṣā hṛtās tasya bhavanti balavardhanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44"><label>4.33.44</label> prāgapītaṃ naraṃ śodhyaṃ pāyayetauṣadhaṃ
            mṛdu |
            <caesura/>
             tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45"><label>4.33.45</label> sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaphalaṃ hṛdyamalpamātraṃ
            mahāguṇam |
            <caesura/>
             vyāpatsvalpātyayaṃ cāpi pibennṛpatirauṣadham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46"><label>4.33.46</label> snehasvedāvanabhyasya yas tu saṃśodhanaṃ
            pibet |
            <caesura/>
             dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehas tasya viśīryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47"><label>4.33.47</label> snehasvedapracalitā rasaiḥ snigdhair
            udīritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhā hartuṃ viśodhanaiḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ
            nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1"><label>4.34.1</label> athāto vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"><label>4.34.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3"><label>4.34.3</label> vaidyāturanimittaṃ vamanaṃ virecanaṃ ca
            pañcadaśadhā vyāpadyate | tatra vamanasyādho gatirūrdhvaṃ virecanasyeti pṛthak;
            sāmānyamubhayoḥ sāvaśeṣaudhatvaṃ, jīrṇauṣadhatvaṃ, hīnadoṣāpahṛtatvaṃ, vātaśūlam, ayogo,
            atiyogo, jīvādānam, ādhmānaṃ, parikartikā, parisrāvaḥ, pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇaṃ,
            vibandha, aṅgapragraha iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4"><label>4.34.4</label> tatra
            bubhukṣāpīḍitasyātitīkṣṇāgnermṛdukoṣṭhasya cāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ durvamasya vā
            guṇasāmānyabhāvādvamanamadho gacchati, tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣotkleśaś ca<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>; tamāśu snehayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair
            vāmayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5"><label>4.34.5</label> apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ
            saśeṣānnasya vā 'hṛdyamatiprabhūtaṃ vā virecanaṃ pītamūrdhvaṃ gacchati,
            tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣokleśaś ca; tatrāśuddhāmāśayamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu vāmayitvā
            bhūyastīkṣṇatarair virecayet, āmānvaye tvāmavat saṃvidhānam, ahṛdye 'tiprabhūte ca
            hṛdyaṃ pramāṇayuktaṃ ca; ata ūrdhvamuttiṣṭhatyauṣadhe na tṛtīyaṃ pāyayet, tatastvenaṃ
            madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktair lehair virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6"><label>4.34.6</label>
            doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadhamavasthitamūrdhvabhāgikamadhobhāgikaṃ vā na sraṃsayati doṣān,
            tatra tṛṣṇā pārśvaśūlaṃ chardirmūrcchā parvabhedo hṛllāso 'ratirudgārāviśuddhiś ca
            bhavati; tamuṣṇābhir adbhir āśu vāmayed ūrdhvabhāgike, adhobhāgike 'pi ca
            sāvaśeṣauṣadhamatipradhāvitadoṣamatibalamasamyagviriktalakṣaṇamapyevaṃ vāmayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7"><label>4.34.7</label>
            krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgneralpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ vā bhaktavat pākam upaiti, tatra
            samudīrṇā doṣā yathākālamanirhrīyamāṇā vyādhivibhramaṃ balavibhraṃśaṃ cāpādayanti,
            tamanalpamamandamauṣadhaṃ ca pāyayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8"><label>4.34.8</label> asnigdhasvinnenālpaguṇaṃ vā bheṣajam
            upayuktamalpān doṣān hanti; tatra vamane doṣaśeṣo gauravamutkleśaṃ hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ
            vyādhivṛddhiṃ ca karoti, tatra taṃ yathāyogaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayed dṛḍhataraṃ; virecane tu
            gudaparikartanamādhmānaṃ śirogauravamaniḥsaraṇaṃ vā vāyor vyādhivṛddhiṃ ca karoti; tam
            upapādya bhūyaḥ snehasvedābhyāṃ virecayed dṛḍhataraṃ, dṛḍhaṃ bahupracalitadoṣaṃ vā
            tṛtīye divase 'lpaguṇaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9"><label>4.34.9</label> asnigdhasvinnena rūkṣauṣadham
            upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā vāyuṃ kopayati, tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ
            pārśvapṛṣṭhaśroṇimanyāmarmaśūlaṃ mūrcchāṃ bhramaṃ madaṃ saṃjñānāśaṃ ca karoti, taṃ
            vātaśūlamity ācakṣate; tamabhyajya dhāvyasvedena svedayitvā yaṣṭīmadhukavipakvena
            tailenānuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10"><label>4.34.10</label> snehasvedābhyām
            avibhāvitaśarīreṇālpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ vā pītamūrdhvamadho vā nābhyeti doṣāṃścotkleśya
            taiḥ saha balakṣayam āpādayati, tatrādhmānaṃ hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇā mūrcchā dāhaś ca bhavati,
            tam ayogamity ācakṣate; tamāśu vāmayenmadanaphalalavaṇāmbubhir virecayet tīkṣṇataraiḥ
            kaṣāyaiś ca | durvāntasya tu samutkliṣṭādoṣā vyāpya śarīraṃ
            kaṇḍūśvayathukuṣṭhapiḍakājvarāṅgamardanistodanāni kurvanti,
            tatastānaśeṣānmadauṣadhenāpaharet | asnigdhasvinnasya durviriktasyādhonābheḥ
            stabdhapūrṇodaratā śūlaṃ vātapurīṣasaṅgaḥ kaṇḍūmaṇḍalaprādurbhāvo vā bhavati,
            tamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsrehya virecayet tīkṣṇena | nātipravartamāne tiṣṭhati vā
            duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārthamuṣṇodakaṃ pāyayet, pāṇitāpaiś ca pārśvodaram
            upasvedayet, tataḥ pravartante doṣāḥ | anupravṛtte cālpadoṣe jīrṇauṣadhaṃ
            bahudoṣamahaḥśeṣaṃ daśarātrādūrdhvam upasaṃskṛtadehaṃ snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayet |
            durvirecyamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsnehya virecayet | hrībhayalobhair vegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥ
            striyo rājasamīpasthā vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś ca bhavanti, tasmād ete durvirecyāḥ,
            bahuvātatvāt ; ata eva tānatisnigdhān svedopapannāñ śodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11"><label>4.34.11</label> sngidhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasya vā
            'titīkṣṇamadhikaṃ vā dattamauṣadhamatiyogaṃ kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge
            pittātipravṛttirbalavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān bhavati, taṃ ghṛtenābhyajyāvagāhya
            śītāsvapsu śarkarāmadhumiśrair lehair upacaredyathāsvaṃ; virecanātiyoge
            kaphasyātipravṛttiruttarakālaṃ ca saraktasya, tatrāpi balavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān
            bhavati, tamatiśītāmbubhiḥ pariṣicyāvagāhya vā śītais taṇḍulāmbubhir
            madhumiśraiśchardayet, picchābastiṃ cāsmai dadyāt, kṣīrasarpiṣā cainamanuvāsayet,
            priyaṅgvādiṃ cāsmai taṇḍulāmbunā pātuṃ prayacchet, kṣīrarasayoś cānyatareṇa bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12"><label>4.34.12</label> tasiminn eva vamanātiyoge pravṛddhe śoṇitaṃ
            ṣṭhīvati chardayati vā, tatra jihvāniḥsaraṇamapasaraṇamakṣṇorvyāvṛttirhanusaṃhananaṃ
            tṛṣṇā hikkā jvaro vaisaṃjñyamity aupadravā bhavanti;
            tamajāsṛkcandanośīrāñjanalājacūrṇaiḥ saśarkarodakair manthaṃ pāyayet, phalarasair vā
            saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaraiḥ śuṅgābhir vā vaṭādīnāṃ peyāṃ siddhāṃ sakṣaudrāṃ varcogrāhibhir
            vā, payasā jāṅgalarasena vā bhojayet , atisrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret; jihvāmatisarpitāṃ
            kaṭukalavaṇacūrṇapraghṛṣṭāṃ tiladrākṣāpraliptāṃ vā 'ntaḥ pīḍayet, antaḥ
            praviṣṭāyāmamlamanye tasya purastāt khādayeyuḥ; vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī ghṛtābhyakte pīḍayet,
            tṛṣṇādiṣu ca yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta, visaṃjñe veṇuvīṇāgītasvanaṃ śrāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13"><label>4.34.13</label> virecanātiyoge ca sacandrakaṃ salilamadhaḥ
            sravati tato māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitaṃ ca, tato gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ
            vepathurvamanātiyogopadravāś cāsya bhavanti; tam api niḥsrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret,
            niḥsarpitagudasya gudamabhyajya parisvedyāntaḥ pīḍayet kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ vā vīkṣeta,
            vepathau vātavyādhividhānaṃ kurvīta, jihvāniḥsaraṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ, atipravṛtte vā
            jīvaśoṇite kāśmarīphalabadarīdūrvośīraiḥ śṛtena payasā ghṛtamaṇḍāñjanayuktena
            suśītenāsthāpayet, nyagrodhādikaṣāyekṣurasaghṛtaśoṇitasaṃsṛṣṭaiś cainaṃ bastibhir
            upācaret, śoṇitaṣṭhīvane raktapittaraktātīsārakriyāś cāsya vidhadhyāt, nyagrodhādiṃ
            cāsya vidadhyāt pānabhojaneṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14"><label>4.34.14</label> jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayoś ca jijñāsārthaṃ
            tasmin picuṃ plotaṃ vā kṣipet, yadyuṣṇodakaprakṣālitam api vastraṃ rañjayati
            tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyaṃ; sabhaktaṃ ca śune dadyācchaktusaṃmiśraṃ vā, sa
            yadyupabhuñjīta tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyam; anyathā raktapittam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15"><label>4.34.15</label> saśeṣānnena bahudoṣeṇa
            rūkṣeṇānilaprāyakoṣṭhenānuṣṇamasnigdhaṃ vā pītamauṣadhamādhmāpayati,
            tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo gudabastinistodanaṃ
            bhaktāruciś ca bhavati, taṃ cādhmānamity ācakṣate; tam
            upasvedyānāhavartidīpanabastikriyābhir upacaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16"><label>4.34.16</label> kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena mandāgninā rūkṣeṇa vā
            'titīkṣṇoṣṇātilavaṇamatirūkṣaṃ vā pītamauṣadhaṃ pittānilau pradūṣya parikartikām
            āpādayati, tatra gudanābhimeḍhrebastiśiraḥsu sadāhaṃ parikartanam anilasaṅgo
            vāyuviṣṭambho bhaktāruciś ca bhavati; tatra picchābastir
            yaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilakalkamadhughṛtayuktaḥ, śītāmbupariṣiktaṃ cainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ
            ghṛtamaṇḍena yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailena vā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17"><label>4.34.17</label> krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadopasya
            mṛdvauṣadhamavacāritaṃ samutkliśya doṣānna niḥśeṣānapaharati, tataste doṣāḥ parisrāvam
            āpādayanti, tatra daurbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucigātrasadanāni bhavanti, savedanau cāsya
            pittaśleṣmāṇau parisravataḥ, taṃ parisrāvamity ācakṣate;
            tamajakarṇadhavatiniśapalāśabalākaṣāyair madhusaṃyuktair āsthāpayet, upaśāntadoṣaṃ
            snigdhaṃ ca bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18"><label>4.34.18</label> atirūkṣe 'tisnigdhe vā <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>bheṣajamavacāritamaprāptaṃ vātavarca
            udīrayati vegāghātena vā, tadā pravāhikā bhavati; tatra savātaṃ sadāhaṃ saśūlaṃ guru
            picchilaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ saraktaṃ vā bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ kapham upaviśati; tāṃ
            parisrāvavidhānenopacaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19"><label>4.34.19</label> yastūrdhvamadho vā bheṣajavegaṃ
            pravṛttamajñatvād vinihanti tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvanti doṣāḥ, tatra
            pradhānamarmasantāpādvedanābhir atyarthaṃ pīḍyamāno dantān kiṭakiṭāyate <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>udgatākṣo jihvāṃ svādati pratāmyatyacetāś ca
            bhavati, taṃ parivarjayanti mūrkhāḥ; tamabhyajya dhānyasvedena svedayet,
            yaṣṭimadhukasiddhena ca tailenānuvāsayet, śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai tīkṣṇaṃ vidadhyāt, tato
            yaṣṭimadhukamiśreṇa taṇḍulāmbunā chardayet, yathādoṣocchrāyeṇa cainaṃ bastibhir upācaret
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20"><label>4.34.20</label> yastūrdhvamadho vā pravṛttadoṣaḥ
            śītāgāramudakamanilamanyadvā seveta, tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥsvavalīyamānā <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>ghānībhāvamāpannā vātamūtraśakṛdgrahamāpādya
            vibadhyante, tasyāṭopo dāho jvaro vedanāś ca tīvrā bhavanti; tamāśu vāmayitvā
            prāptakālāṃ kriyāṃ kurvīta; adhobhāge tvadhobhāgadoṣaharadravyaṃ
            saindhavāmlamūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ virecanāya pāyayet, āsthāpanamanuvāsanaṃ ca yathādoṣaṃ
            vidadhyāt, yathādoṣamāhārakramaṃ ca; ubhayatobhāge tūpadravaviśeṣān yathāsvaṃ
            pratikurvīta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21"><label>4.34.21</label> yā tu virecane gudaparikartikā tadvamane
            kaṇṭhakṣaṇanaṃ, yadadhaḥ parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrdhvabhāge śleṣmaprasekaḥ, yā tvadhāḥ
            pravāhikā sā tūrdhvaṃ śuṣkodgārā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22"><label>4.34.22</label> bhavati cātra
            <caesura/>
             yās tv etā vyāpadaḥ proktā daśa pañca ca tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             etā virekātiyogaduryogāyogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ nāma
            catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||34 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="35" type="adhyāya">

          <head>pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

          <milestone unit="folio" n="dscn3276 fol 297"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.1"><label>4.35.1</label> athāto netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.2"><label>4.35.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.3"><label>4.35.3</label> tatra snehādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ bastikarma
            pradhānatamamāhurācāryāḥ | kasmāt anekakarmakaratvād basteḥ; iha khalu bastir
            nānāvidhadravyasaṃyogāddoṣāṇāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṃgrahaṇāni karoti, kṣīṇaśukraṃ
            vājīkaroti, kṛśaṃ bṛṃhayati, sthūlaṃ karśayati, cakṣuḥ prīṇayati, valīpalitamapahanti,
            vayaḥ sthāpayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.4"><label>4.35.4</label> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
            <caesura/>
             kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.5"><label>4.35.5</label> tathā
              jvarātīsāratimirapratiśyāyaśirorogādhimanthārditākṣepakapakṣāghātaikāṅgasarvāṅgarogādhmānodarayoniśūlaśarkarāśūlavṛddhyupadaṃśānāhamūtrakṛcchragulmavātaśoṇitavātamūtrapurīṣodāvartaśukrārtavastanyanāśahṛddhanumanyāgrahaśarkarāśmarīmūḍhagarbhaprabhṛtiṣu<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> cāsyartham upayujyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.6"><label>4.35.6</label> bhavati cātra
            <caesura/>
             bastir vāte ca pitte ca kaphe rakte ca śasyate |
            <caesura/>
             saṃsarge sannipāte ca bastir eva hitaḥ sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.7"><label>4.35.7</label> tatra sāṃvatsarikāṣṭadviraṣṭavarṣāṇāṃ
            ṣaḍaṣṭadaśāṅgulapramāṇāni kaniṣṭhikānāmikāmadhyamāṅgulipariṇāhānyagre
            'dhyardhāṅguladvyaṅgulārdhatṛtīyāṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikāni
            kaṅkaśyenabarhiṇapakṣanāḍītulyapraveśāni mudgamāṣakalāyamātrasrotāṃsi vidadhyānnetrāṇi |
            teṣu cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇamāturahastasaṃmitena prasṛtena saṃmitau prasṛtau dvau
            catvāro 'ṣṭau ca vidheyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.8"><label>4.35.8</label> varṣāntareṣu netrāṇāṃ bastimānasya caiva hi |
            <caesura/>
             vayobalaśarīrāṇi samīkṣyotkarṣayed vidhim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.9"><label>4.35.9</label> pañcaviṃśaterūrdhvaṃ dvādaśāṅgulaṃ, mūle
            'ṅguṣṭhodaraparīṇāham, agre kaniṣṭhikodaraparīṇāham, agre tryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikaṃ,
            gṛdhrapakṣanāḍīṃtulyapraveśaṃ, kolāsthimātrachidraṃ, klinnakalāyamātrachidramity eke;
            sarvāṇi mūle bastinibandhanārthaṃ dvikarṇikāni | āsthāpanadravyapraṇāṇaṃ tu vihitaṃ
            dvādaśaprasṛtāḥ | saptatestūrdhvaṃ netrapramāṇametadeva, dravyapramāṇaṃ tu
            dviraṣṭavarṣavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.10"><label>4.35.10</label> mṛdurbastiḥ prayoktavyo
            viśeṣādbālavṛddhayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tayostīkṣṇaḥ prayuktas tu bastir hiṃsyād balāyuṣī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.11"><label>4.35.11</label> (vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ mudgavāhisrotaḥ;
            vraṇamavekṣya yathāsvaṃ snehakaṣāye vidadhīta ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.12"><label>4.35.12</label> tatra netrāṇi suvarṇarajatatāmrāyor
            ītidantaśṛṅgamaṇitarusāramayāni ślakṣṇāni dṛḍhāni gopucchākṛtīnyṛjūni guṭikāmukhāni ca
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.13"><label>4.35.13</label> bastayaś ca <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>bandhyā mṛdavo nātivahalā dṛḍhāḥ
            pramāṇavanto gomahiṣavarāhājorabhrāṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.14"><label>4.35.14</label> netrālābhe hitā nāḍī nalavaṃśāsthisaṃbhavā
            |
            <caesura/>
             bastyalābhe hitaṃ carma sūkṣmaṃ vā tāntavaṃ ghanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.15"><label>4.35.15</label> bastiṃ nirupadigdhaṃ tu śuddhaṃ
            suparimārjitam |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdvanuddhatahīnaṃ ca muhuḥ snehavimarditam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.16"><label>4.35.16</label> netrāmūle pratiṣṭhāpya nyubjaṃ tu
            vivṛtānanam |
            <caesura/>
             baddhvā lohena taptena carmasrotasi nirdahet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.17"><label>4.35.17</label> parivartya tato bastiṃ baddhvā guptaṃ
            nidhāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ ca tailaṃ ca yathāvattena dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.18"><label>4.35.18</label> tatra dvividho bastiḥ nairūhikaḥ, snaihikaś
            ca | āsthāpanaṃ, nirūha ity anarthāntaraṃ; tasya vikalpo mādhutailikaḥ; tasya
            prayāyaśabdo yāpano, yuktarathaḥ, siddhabastir iti | sa doṣanirharaṇāccharīranīrohaṇādvā
            nirūhaḥ, bayaḥsthāpanādāyuḥsthāpanādvā āsthāpanam | mādhutailikavidhānaṃ ca
            nirūhopakramacikitsite vakṣyāmaḥ | yathāpramāṇaguṇavihitaḥ snehabastivikalpo 'nuvāsanaḥ
            pādāva(pādāpa)kṛṣṭaḥ | anuvasannapi na duṣyatyanudivasaṃ vā dīyata ity anuvāsanaḥ |
            tasyāpi vikalpo+ardhārdhamātrāvakṛṣṭo 'parihāryo mātrābastir iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.19"><label>4.35.19</label> nirūhaḥ śodhano lekhī snaihiko bṛṃhaṇo
            mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nirūhaśodhitānmārgān samyak sneho 'nugacchati |
            <caesura/>
             apetasarvadoṣāsu nāḍīṣv iva vahajjalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.20"><label>4.35.20</label> sarvadoṣaharaś cāsau śarīrasya ca jīvanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmād viśuddhadehasya snehabastir vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.21"><label>4.35.21</label> tatronmāda<pc> </pc>bhaya<pc
              > </pc>śoka<pc> </pc>pipāsārocakājīrṇārśaḥ<pc> </pc>pāṇḍuroga<pc
              > </pc>bhrama<pc> </pc>mada<pc> </pc>mūrcchā<pc> </pc>cchardi<pc
              > </pc>kuṣṭha<pc> </pc>mehodarasthaulya<pc> </pc>śvāsa<pc> </pc>kāsa<pc
              > </pc>kaṇṭhaśoṣa<pc> </pc>śophopasṛṣṭa<pc> </pc>kṣata<pc> </pc>kṣīṇa<pc
            > </pc>catustrimāsagarbhiṇīdurbalāgnyasahā bālavṛddhau ca vātarogādṛte kṣīṇā nānuvāsyā
            nāsthāpayitavyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.22"><label>4.35.22</label> udarī ca pramehī ca kuṣṭhī sthūlaś ca
            mānavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             avaśyaṃ sthāpanīyāste nānuvāsyāḥ kathañcana || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.23"><label>4.35.23</label> asādhyatā vikārāṇāṃ syād eṣāmanuvāsanāt |
            <caesura/>
             asādhyatve 'pi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.24"><label>4.35.24</label> pakvāśaye tathā śroṇyāṃ nābhyadhastāc ca
            sarvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             samyakpraṇihito bastiḥ sthāneṣveteṣu tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.25"><label>4.35.25</label> pakvāśayādbastivīryaṃ khair deham
            anusarpati |
            <caesura/>
             vṛkṣamūle niṣiktānāmapāṃ vīryamiva drumam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.26"><label>4.35.26</label> sa cāpi sahasā bastiḥ kevalaḥ samalo 'pi vā
            |
            <caesura/>
             pratyeti vīryaṃ tvanilair apānādyair vinīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.27"><label>4.35.27</label> vīryeṇa bastirādatte doṣānāpādamastakāt(n)
            |
            <caesura/>
             pakvāśayastho 'mbarago bhūmerarko rasāniva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.28"><label>4.35.28</label> sa kaṭīpṛṣṭhakoṣṭhasthān vīryeṇāloḍya
            saṃcayān |
            <caesura/>
             utkhātamūlān harati doṣāṇāṃ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.29"><label>4.35.29</label> doṣatrayasya yasmāc ca prakope vāyurīśvaraḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt tasyātivṛddhasya śarīram abhinighnataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.30"><label>4.35.30</label> vāyor viṣahate vegaṃ nānyā basterṛte kriyā
            |
            <caesura/>
             pavanāviddhatoyasya velā vegamivodadheḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.31"><label>4.35.31</label> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.32"><label>4.35.32</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ vyāpado vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra
            netraṃ vicalitaṃ, vivartitaṃ, pārśvāvapīḍitam, atyutkṣiptam, avasannaṃ, tiryakprakṣiptam
            iti ṣaṭ praṇidhānadoṣāḥ; atisthūlaṃ, karkaśam, avanataṃ, aṇubhinnaṃ,
            sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭakarṇikaṃ, sūkṣmāticchidram, atidīrgham, <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>atihrasvam, asrimadity ekādaśa netradoṣāḥ;
            bahalatā, alpatā, sacchidratā, prastīrṇatā, durbaddhateti pañca bastidoṣāḥ; atipīḍitatā,
            śithilapīḍitatā, bhūyo bhūyo 'vapīḍanaṃ, kālātikrama iti catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ; āmatā,
            hīnatā, atimātratā, atiśītatā, atyuṣṇatā, atitīkṣṇatā, atimṛdutā, atisnigdhatā,
            atirūkṣatā, atisāndratā, atidravatā, ity ekādaśa dravyadoṣāḥ;
            avākśīrṣocchīrṣanyubjottānasaṅkucitadehasthitadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinaḥ pradānam iti sapta
            śayyādoṣāḥ; evam etāś catuś catvāriṃśadvyāpado vaidyanimittāḥ | āturanimittāḥ pañcadaśa
            āturopadravacikitsite vakṣyante | snehastvaṣṭabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ pratihato na pratyāgacchati
            tribhir doṣaiḥ, aśanābhibhūto, malavyāmiśro, dūrānupraviṣṭo, asvinnasya, anuṣṇo,
            alpambhuktavato, alpaś ceti vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ayogastūbhayoḥ, ādhmānaṃ,
            parikartikā, parisrāvaḥ, pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇam, aṅgapragraho, atiyogo, jīvādānam
            iti nava vyāpado vaidyanimittā bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.33"><label>4.35.33</label> bhavati cātra ṣaṭsaptatiḥ samāsena vyāpadaḥ
            parikīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiṃ ca tadanantaram ||</l>

            netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitstitaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35 ||</p>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.39"><label>4.36.39</label> parisravettataḥ pittaṃ dāhaṃ sañjanayed
            gude |

             dattas tu prathamo bastiḥ snehayed bastivaṅkṣaṇau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.72"><label>4.37.72</label> samyagdatto dvitīyas tu mūrdhasthamanilaṃ

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.73"><label>4.37.73</label> rasaṃ caturtho raktaṃ tu pañcamaḥ snehayet
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṣṭhas tu snehayenmāṃsaṃ medaḥ saptama eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.74"><label>4.37.74</label> aṣṭamo navamaś cāsthi majjānaṃ ca

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.77"><label>4.37.77</label> snehabastiṃ nirūhaṃ vā naikamevātiśīlayet |

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.1"><label>4.38.1</label> athāto nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.2"><label>4.38.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.3"><label>4.38.3</label> athānuvāsitamāsthāpayet;
            svabhyaktasvinnaśarīramutsṛṣṭabahirvegamavāte śucau veśmani madhyāhne pratatāyāṃ
            śayyāyāmadhaḥsuparigrahāyāṃ śroṇipradeśaprativyūḍhāyāmanupadhānāyāṃ
            vāmapārśvaśāyinamākuñcitadakṣiṇasakthimitaraprasāritasakthiṃ sumanasaṃ jīrṇānnaṃ
            vāgyataṃ suniṣaṇṇadehaṃ viditvā, tato vāmapādasyopari netraṃ
            kṛtvetarapādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ karṇikām upari niṣpīḍya, savyapāṇikaniṣṭhikānāmikābhyāṃ
            bastermukhārdhaṃ saṅkocya, madhyamāpradeśinyaṅguṣṭhair ardhaṃ<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> tu vivṛtāsyaṃ kṛtvā, bastāvauṣadhaṃ
            prakṣipya, dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhena pradeśinīmadhyamābhyāṃ
            cānusiktamanāyatamabudbudamasaṅkucitamavātamauṣadhāsannam upasaṃgṛhya<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>, punarupari taditareṇa gṛhītvā
            dakṣiṇenāvasiñcet, tataḥ sūtreṇaivauṣadhānte dvistrirvā++āveṣṭya badhnīyāt, atha
            dakṣiṇenottānena pāṇinā bastiṃ gṛhītvā vāmahastamadhyamāṅgulipradeśinībhyāṃ netram
            upasaṃgṛhyāṅguṣṭena netradvāraṃ pidhāya, ghṛtābhyaktāgranetraṃ ghṛtāktamupādāya
            prayacched anupṛṣṭhavaṃśaṃ samamunmukhamākarṇikaṃ netraṃ praṇidhatsveti brūyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.4"><label>4.38.4</label> bastiṃ savye kare kṛtvā dakṣiṇenāvapīḍayet |
            <caesura/>
             ekenaivāvapīḍena na drutaṃ na vilambitam || </l>

            bhavati || </l>
