        <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1"><label>4.40.1</label> athāto dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"><label>4.40.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3"><label>4.40.3</label> dhūmaḥ pañcavidho bhavati tad yathā
            prāyogikaḥ, snaihiko, vair enikaḥ, kāsaghno, vāmanīyaś ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4"><label>4.40.4</label> tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena
            ślakṣṇapiṣṭena dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍamaṅgulipariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ veṣṭayitvā
            lepayed eṣā vartiḥ prāyogike, snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiḥ
            snehamiśraiḥ snaihike, śirovirecanadravyair vair ecane,
            bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukāsamardahiṅgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭaśṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
            kāsaharaiś ca kāsaghne,
            snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭakāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakṛmiprabhṛtibhir vāmanīyaiś ca
            vāmanīye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5"><label>4.40.5</label> tatra bastinetradravyair dhūmanetradravyāṇi
            vyākhyātāni bhavanti | dhūmanetraṃ tu kaniṣṭhikāpariṇāhamagre kalāyamātrasroto mūle
            'ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ dhūmavartipraveśasroto 'ṅgulānyaṣṭacatvāriṃśat prāyogike, dvātriṃśat
            snehane, caturviṃśatirvair ecane, ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ kāsaghne vāmanīye ca | ete 'pi
            kolāsthimātracchidre bhavataḥ | vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ vraṇadhūpanārthaṃ
            kalāyaparimaṇḍalaṃ kulatthavāhisrota iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6"><label>4.40.6</label> atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā
            ṛjvadhodṛṣṭiratandritaḥ sthire samāhite śarāve prakṣipya vartiṃ mūlacchidreṇānyena
            śarāveṇa pidhāya tasmin chidre netramūlaṃ saṃyojya dhūmamāseveta, praśānte dhūme
            vartimavaśiṣṭāṃ prakṣipya punarapi dhūmaṃ pāyayed ādoṣaviśuddheḥ; eṣa
            dhūmapānopāyavidhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11"><label>4.40.11</label> tatra
            śokaśramabhayāmarṣauṣṇyaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchādāhapipāsāpāṇḍurogatāluśoṣacchardiśiro
            'bhighātodgārāpatarpitatimirapramehodarādhmānordhvavātārtā
            bālavṛddhadurbalaviriktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣīṇakṣatoraskamadhughṛtad
            adhidugdhamatsyamadyayavāgūpītālpakaphāś ca na dhūmamāseveran || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12"><label>4.40.12</label> akālapītaḥ kurute bhramaṃ mūrcchāṃ
            śirorujam |
            <caesura/>
             ghrāṇaśrotrākṣijihvānām upaghātaṃ ca dāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13"><label>4.40.13</label> ādyās tu trayo dhūmā dvādaśasu
            kāleṣūpādeyāḥ | tad yathā
            kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanadivāsvapnamaithunacchardimūtroccārahasitaruṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv
            iti | tatra vibhāgo mūtroccārakṣavathuhasitaruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ,
            snānacchardivāsvapnānteṣu vair ecanikaḥ, dantaprakṣālanasya snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu
            prāyogika iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14"><label>4.40.14</label> tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati, snehād
            upalepāc ca; vair ecanaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśyāpakarṣati,
            raukṣyāttaikṣṇyādauṣṇyādvaiśadyācca; prāyogikaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśayatyutkliṣṭaṃ
            cāpakarṣati śamayati vātaṃ sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15"><label>4.40.15</label> bhavati cātra naro dhūmopayogācca
            prasannendriyavāṅmanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dṛḍhakeśadvijaśmaśruḥ sugandhiviśadānanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16"><label>4.40.16</label> tathā
            kāsaśvāsārocakāsyopalepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrathatandrānidrāhanumanyāstambhāḥ
            pīnasaśirorogakarṇākṣiśūlā vātakaphanimittāś cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17"><label>4.40.17</label> tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatra yogo rogapraśamanaḥ, ayogo rogāpraśamanaḥ,
              tālugalaśoṣaparidāhapipāsāmūrcchābhramamadakarṇakṣveḍadṛṣṭināsārogadaurbalyānyatiyogo<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> janayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18"><label>4.40.18</label> prāyogikaṃ trīṃstrīnucchvāsānādadīta
            mukhanāsikābhyāṃ ca paryāyāṃstrīṃś caturo veti, snaihikaṃ yāvadaśrupravṛttiḥ, vair
            ecanikamādoṣadarśanāt, tilataṇḍulayavāgūpītena pātavyo vāmanīyaḥ, grāsāntareṣu kāsaghna
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19"><label>4.40.19</label> vraṇadhūmaṃ śarāvasaṃpuṭopanītena netreṇa
            vraṇam ānayet, dhūmapānādvedanopaśamo vraṇavaiśadyam āsrāvopaśamaś ca bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20"><label>4.40.20</label> vidhireṣa samāsena dhūmasyābhihito mayā |
            <caesura/>
             nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ niravaśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21"><label>4.40.21</label> auṣadhamauṣadhasiddho vā sneho nāsikābhyāṃ
            dīyata iti nasyam | tad dvividhaṃ śirovirecanaṃ, snehanaṃ ca | tad dvividham api
            pañcadhā | tad yathā nasyaṃ, śirovirecanaṃ, pratimarśo, avapīḍaḥ, pradhamanaṃ ca | teṣu
            nasyaṃ pradhānaṃ śirovirecanaṃ ca; nasyavikalpaḥ pratimarśaḥ, śirovirecanavikalpo
            'vapīḍaḥ pradhamanaṃ ca; tato nasyaśabdaḥ pañcadhā niyamitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22"><label>4.40.22</label> tatra yaḥ snehanārthaṃ śūnyaśirasāṃ
            grīvāskandhorasāṃ ca balajananārthaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādajananārthaṃ vā sneho vidhīyate tasmin
            vaiśeṣiko nasyaśabdaḥ | tat tu deyaṃ vātābhibhūte śirasi
            dantakeśaśmaśruprapātadāruṇakarṇaśūlakarṇakṣveḍatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogāsyaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprādurbhāvadāruṇaprabodheṣu
            vātapaittikeṣu mukharogeṣv anyeṣu ca vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23"><label>4.40.23</label> śirovirecanaṃ śleṣmaṇā
            'bhivyāptatālukaṇṭhaśirasāmarocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasārdhāvabhedakakṛmipratiśyāyāpasmāragandhājñāneṣv
            anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu kaphajeṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyais tatsiddhena vā
            sneheneti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24"><label>4.40.24</label> tatraitaddvividhamapyabhuktavato 'nnakāle
            pūrvāhṇe śleṣmarogiṇāṃ, madhyāhne pittarogiṇāṃ, aparāhṇe vātarogiṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25"><label>4.40.25</label> atha puruṣāya śirovirecanīyāya
            tyaktamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle dantakāṣṭhadhūmapānābhyāṃ
            viśuddhavaktrasrotase pāṇitāpaparisvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne
            veśmanyuttānaśāyine prasāritakaracaraṇāya kiñcit pravilambitaśirase
            vastrācchāditanetrāya vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotasi
            dakṣiṇahastena sneham uṣṇāmbunā prataptaṃ rajatasuvarṇatāmramaṇimṛtpātraśuktīnām
            anyatamasthaṃ śuktyā picunā vā sukhoṣṇaṃ snehamadrutam āsiñced avyavacchinnadhāraṃ yathā
            netre na prāpnoti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26"><label>4.40.26</label> snehe 'vasicyamāne tu śiro naiva
            prakampayet |
            <caesura/>
             na kupyen na prabhāṣec ca na kṣuyān na haset tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27"><label>4.40.27</label> etair hi vihataḥ sneho na samyak
            pratipadyate |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ kāsapratiśyāyaśiro 'kṣigadasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28"><label>4.40.28</label> tasya pramāṇamaṣtau bindavaḥ
            pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsṛtāḥ prathamā mātrā, dvitīyā śuktiḥ, tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktiḥ, ity
            etāstisro mātrā yathābalaṃ prayojyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"><label>4.40.29</label> snehanasyaṃ nopagilet kathaṃ cid api
            buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30"><label>4.40.30</label> śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti vadanād yathā
            |
            <caesura/>
             kaphotkleśabhayāccainaṃ niṣṭhīvedavidhārayan || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31"><label>4.40.31</label> datte ca punarapi saṃsvedya galakapolādīn
            dhūmamāseveta, bhojayeccainam abhiṣyandi, tato 'syācārikam ādiśet;
            rajodhūmasnehātapamadyadravapānaśiraḥsnānātiyānakrodhādīni ca pariharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32"><label>4.40.32</label> tasya yogātiyogāyogānāmidaṃ vijñānaṃ
            bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33"><label>4.40.33</label> lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge sukhasvapnaprabodhanam
            |
            <caesura/>
             vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhirindiryāṇāṃ manaḥsukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34"><label>4.40.34</label> kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             lakṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnayatisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ tatrāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"><label>4.40.35</label> ayoge vātavaiguṇyamindriyāṇāṃ ca rūkṣatā |
            rogāśāntiś ca tatreṣṭaṃ bhūyo nasyaṃ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36"><label>4.40.36</label> catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā tathā 'ṣṭau vā
            yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             śirovirekasnehasya pramāṇam abhinirdiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37"><label>4.40.37</label> nasye trīṇyupadiṣṭāni lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             śuddha(śuddhi)hīnātisaṃjñāni viśeṣācchāstracintakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38"><label>4.40.38</label> lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ suddhiḥ srotasāṃ
            vyādhinirjayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cittendriyaprasādaś ca śirasaḥ śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39"><label>4.40.39</label> kaṇḍūpadehau gurutā srotasāṃ kaphasaṃsravaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             mūrdhni hīnaviśuddhe tu lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40"><label>4.40.40</label> mastuluṅgāgamo vātavṛddhirindriyavibhramaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41"><label>4.40.41</label> hīnātiśuddhe śirasi kaphavātaghnam ācaret |
            <caesura/>
             samyagviśuddhe śirasi sarpirnasyaṃ niṣecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42"><label>4.40.42</label> (ekāntaraṃ dvyanataraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā punaḥ
            punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ekaviṃśatirātraṃ vā yāvadvā sādhu manyate ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"><label>4.40.43</label> mārutenābhibhūtasya vā 'tyantaṃ yasya
            dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dvikālaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ nasyaṃ tasya vijānatā ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"><label>4.40.44</label> avapīḍastu
            śirovirecanavadabhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭavisaṃjñebhyo dadyāc chirocirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam
            avapiṣyāvapīḍya ca,</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a"><label>4.40.44a</label> śarkarekṣurasakṣīraghṛtamāṃsarasānām
            anyatamaṃ kṣīṇānāṃ śoṇitapitte ca vidadhyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"><label>4.40.45</label> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ sukumārasya yoṣitām |
            <caesura/>
             śṛtāḥ snehāḥ śiraḥśuddhyai kalkastebhyo yathā hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"><label>4.40.46</label> cetovikārakṛmiviṣābhipannānāṃ cūrṇaṃ
            pradhamet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47"><label>4.40.47</label> nasyena parihartavyo bhutavānapatarpito
            'tyarthataruṇapratiśyāyī garbhiṇī pītasnehodakamadyadravo 'jīrṇī dattabastiḥ kruddho
            garārtastṛṣitaḥ śokābhibhūtaḥ ānto bālo vṛddho vegāvarodhitaḥ śiraḥsnātukāmaś ceti;
            anārtave cābhre nasyadhūmau pariharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"><label>4.40.48</label> tatra
            hīnātimātrātiśītoṣṇasahasāpradānādatipravilambitaśirasa ucchiṅghato vicalato
            'bhyavaharato vā pratiṣiddhapradānāc ca vyāpado bhavanti tṛṣṇodgārādayo doṣanimittāḥ
            kṣayajāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49"><label>4.40.49</label> bhavataś cātra nasye śirovireke ca vyāpado
            dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣotkleśāt kṣayāccaiva vijñeyāstā yathākramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50"><label>4.40.50</label> doṣokleśanimittās tu jayecchamanaśodhanaiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             atha kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51"><label>4.40.51</label> pratimarśaś caturdaśasu kāleṣūpādeyaḥ; tad
            yathā talpotthitena, prakṣālitadantena, gṛhānnirgacchatā,
            vyāyāmavyavāyādhvapariśrāntena, mūtroccārakavalāñjanānte, bhuktavatā, charditavatā,
            divāsvapnotthitena, sāyaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52"><label>4.40.52</label> tatra talpotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo
            rātrāvupacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ malam upahanti manaḥprasādaṃ ca karoti,
            prakṣālitadantenāsevito dantānāṃ dṛḍhatāṃ vadanasaugandhyaṃ cāpādayati, gṛhānnirgacchatā
            sevito nāsāseotasaḥ klinnatayā rajodhūmo vā na bādhate,
            vyāyāmamaithunādhvapariśrāntenāsevitaḥ śramam upahanti, mūtroccārānte sevito
            dṛṣṭergurutvam apanayati, kavalāñjanānte sevito dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati, bhuktavatā sevitaḥ
            srotasāṃ viśuddhiṃ laghutāṃ cāpādayati, vāntenāsevitaḥ srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇamapohya
            bhaktākāṅkṣām āpādayati, divāsvapnotthitenāsevito nidrāśeṣaṃ gurutvaṃ malaṃ cāpohya
            cittaikāgryaṃ janayati, sāyaṃ cāsevitaḥ sukhanidrāprabodhaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53"><label>4.40.53</label> īṣaducchiṅghataḥ sneho yāvadvaktraṃ
            prapadyate |
            <caesura/>
             nasye niṣiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54"><label>4.40.54</label> nasyena rogāḥ śāmyanti
            narāṇāmūrdhvajatrujāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             indriyāṇāṃ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyaṃ sugandhi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55"><label>4.40.55</label> hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ balam |
            <caesura/>
             valīpalitakhālity avyaṅgānāṃ cāpy asaṃbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"><label>4.40.56</label> tailaṃ kaphe savāte syāt kevale pavane
            vasām |
            <caesura/>
             dadyāt sarpiḥ sadā pitte majjānaṃ ca samārute || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"><label>4.40.57</label> caturvidhasya snehasya vidhirevaṃ
            prakīrtitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailaṃ vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"><label>4.40.58</label> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kavalagrahaṇe vidhim
            |
            <caesura/>
             caturdhā kavalaḥ snehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"><label>4.40.59</label> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte svāduśītaiḥ
            prasādanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pitte kaṭvamlalavaṇai rūkṣoṣṇaiḥ śodhanaḥ kaphe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"><label>4.40.60</label> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇai ropaṇo vraṇe
            |
            <caesura/>
             caturvidhasya caivāsya viśeṣo 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"><label>4.40.61</label> tatra
            trikaṭukavacāsarṣapaharītakīkalkamāloḍya tailaśuktasurāmūtrakṣāramadhūnāmanyatamena
            salavaṇam abhiprataptam upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśo dhārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"><label>4.40.62</label> sukhaṃ saṃcāryate yā tu mātrā sa (sā)
            kavalaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asaṃcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"><label>4.40.63</label> tāvac ca dhārayitavyo
            'nanyamanasonnatadehena yāvaddoṣaparipūrṇakapolatvaṃ nāsāsrotonayanapariplāvaś ca
            bhavati tadā vimoktavyaḥ, punaś cānyo grahītavya iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"><label>4.40.64</label> evaṃ snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmlasaṃbhṛtāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāṃ ca kavalā doṣato hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"><label>4.40.65</label> vyādher apacayastuṣṭirvaiśadyaṃ
            vaktralāghavam |
            <caesura/>
             indiryāṇāṃ prasādaś ca kavale śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"><label>4.40.66</label> hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśāvarasajñānam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             atiyogān mukhe pākaḥ śoṣatṛṣṇāruciklamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67"><label>4.40.67</label> śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavanty eva na saṃśayaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             tilā nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"><label>4.40.68</label> sakṣaudro dagdhavaktrasya gaṇḍūṣo
            dāhanāśanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kavalasya vidhirhyeṣa samāsena prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"><label>4.40.69</label> vibhajya bheṣajaṃ buddhyā kurvīta
            pratisāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇaṃ ceti caturvidham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"><label>4.40.70</label> aṅgulyagrapraṇītaṃ tu yathāsvaṃ
            mukharogiṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tasmin yogamayogaṃ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"><label>4.40.71</label> tān eva śamayed vyādhīn kavalo yān apohati
            |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaghnam anabhiṣyandi bhojayec ca tathā naram ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ nāma
            catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
